function validateDataStructure(data) {
  // 1. åŸºæœ¬æ§‹é€ ã®ç¢ºèª
  if (!data.links || !Array.isArray(data.links)) {
    return { valid: false, error: 'Invalid links structure' };
  }

  // 2. å¿…é ˆãƒ•ã‚£ãƒ¼ãƒ«ãƒ‰ã®ç¢ºèª
  const requiredFields = ['id', 'title', 'type'];
  for (const field of requiredFields) {
    if (!data[field]) {
      return { valid: false, error: `Missing ${field}` };
    }
  }

  // 3. ãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ å›ºæœ‰ã®ç¢ºèª
  const sonyMusic = data.links.find(link => link.platform === 'sony_music');
  if (!sonyMusic) {
    return { valid: false, error: 'Missing sony_music platform' };
  }

  return { valid: true };
}
```

### 3-2. æ¯”è¼ƒãƒ„ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã®ä¾‹
```javascript
function compareData(source, target) {
  // 1. ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®å¯¾å¿œç¢ºèª
  const mapping = new Map();
  source.forEach(item => {
    mapping.set(item.id, item);
  });

  // 2. å·®åˆ†ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
  const differences = [];
  target.forEach(item => {
    const sourceItem = mapping.get(item.id);
    if (!sourceItem) {
      differences.push({ type: 'missing', id: item.id });
      return;
    }
    if (sourceItem.url !== item.url) {
      differences.push({ type: 'mismatch', id: item.id });
    }
  });

  return differences;
}
```

3. æ¬¡ã«ã€å…ƒã®ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‹ã‚‰å¿…è¦ãªãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’æŠ½å‡ºã—ã¦ã€æ­£ã—ã„ãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ æ§‹é€ ã«å¤‰æ›ã™ã‚‹ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

  'rakuma'
];

// ãƒ†ãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ¬ãƒ¼ãƒˆã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿

// å…ƒã®ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿

// æ–°ã—ã„ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®ä½œæˆ

  // ãƒ†ãƒ³ãƒ—ãƒ¬ãƒ¼ãƒˆã®æ§‹é€ ã‚’ã‚³ãƒ”ãƒ¼

  // åŸºæœ¬æƒ…å ±ã®ã‚³ãƒ”ãƒ¼
  newItem.id = item.id;
  newItem.title = item.title;
  newItem.type = item.type;
  newItem.notes = item.notes;
  newItem.categories = item.categories;

  // ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯ã®å‡¦ç†
  newItem.links = newItem.links.map(templateLink => {
    const originalLink = item.links.find(l => l.platform === templateLink.platform);
    if (originalLink) {
      return {
        ...templateLink,
        urls: originalLink.urls
      };
    }
    return templateLink;
  });

  return newItem;
});

// æ–°ã—ã„ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®ä¿å­˜
fs.writeFileSync('../public/data/media-master.json', JSON.stringify(newData, null, 2));

2. URLã®ç¢ºèªã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const csv = require('csv-parse/sync');

// CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
const csvContent = fs.readFileSync('SonyMusicã®å•†å“ä¸€è¦§_VOTE30ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯æ´—ã„å‡ºã—ç”¨.csv', 'utf8');
const records = csv.parse(csvContent, {
  columns: true,
  skip_empty_lines: true
});

// JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
const jsonData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('../public/data/media-master.json', 'utf8'));

// ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã¨URLã®ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°ã‚’ä½œæˆ
const urlMap = new Map();
records.forEach(record => {
  urlMap.set(record.title.trim(), record.url);
});

// çµæœã‚’æ ¼ç´ã™ã‚‹é…åˆ—
const results = [];

// å„JSONã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒªã‚’ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
jsonData.forEach(item => {
  const sonyMusicPlatform = item.links.find(link => link.platform === 'sony_music');
  if (!sonyMusicPlatform) {
    results.push({
      id: item.id,
      title: item.title,
      error: 'sony_musicãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ ãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“'
    });
    return;
  }

  const currentUrl = sonyMusicPlatform.urls.direct;
  const csvUrl = urlMap.get(item.title);

  if (!currentUrl && csvUrl) {
    results.push({
      id: item.id,
      title: item.title,
      error: 'URLãŒæœªè¨­å®šã§ã™',
      expectedUrl: csvUrl
    });
  } else if (currentUrl && !csvUrl) {
    results.push({
      id: item.id,
      title: item.title,
      error: 'CSVã«URLãŒå­˜åœ¨ã—ã¾ã›ã‚“',
      currentUrl: currentUrl
    });
  } else if (currentUrl !== csvUrl && csvUrl) {
    results.push({
      id: item.id,
      title: item.title,
      error: 'URLãŒä¸€è‡´ã—ã¾ã›ã‚“',
      currentUrl: currentUrl,
      expectedUrl: csvUrl
    });
  }
});

// çµæœã®å‡ºåŠ›
if (results.length === 0) {
  console.log('ã™ã¹ã¦ã®URLãŒæ­£ã—ãè¨­å®šã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚');
} else {
  console.log('ä»¥ä¸‹ã®å•é¡ŒãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã—ãŸï¼š\n');
  results.forEach(result => {
    console.log(`ID: ${result.id}`);
    console.log(`ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${result.title}`);
    console.log(`ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: ${result.error}`);
    if (result.currentUrl) console.log(`ç¾åœ¨ã®URL: ${result.currentUrl}`);
    if (result.expectedUrl) console.log(`æœŸå¾…ã•ã‚Œã‚‹URL: ${result.expectedUrl}`);
    console.log('---\n');
  });
}
```

ä¿®æ­£ã—ãŸã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’å®Ÿè¡Œã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

  // CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿

  console.log('CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®å†…å®¹:', csvContent);
  
  const records = parse(csvContent, {
    columns: true,
    skip_empty_lines: true
  });
  console.log('ãƒ‘ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã•ã‚ŒãŸãƒ¬ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰:', records);

  // JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿

      urlMap.set(record.title.trim(), record.url);
    } else {
      console.log('ç„¡åŠ¹ãªãƒ¬ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰:', record);
    }
  });

  // çµæœã‚’æ ¼ç´ã™ã‚‹é…åˆ—

    if (!sonyMusicPlatform) {
      results.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: item.title,
        error: 'sony_musicãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ ãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã›ã‚“'
      });
      return;

    const csvUrl = urlMap.get(item.title);

    if (!currentUrl && csvUrl) {
      results.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: item.title,
        error: 'URLãŒæœªè¨­å®šã§ã™',
        expectedUrl: csvUrl
      });
    } else if (currentUrl && !csvUrl) {
      results.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: item.title,
        error: 'CSVã«URLãŒå­˜åœ¨ã—ã¾ã›ã‚“',
        currentUrl: currentUrl
      });

      results.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: item.title,
        error: 'URLãŒä¸€è‡´ã—ã¾ã›ã‚“',
        currentUrl: currentUrl,
        expectedUrl: csvUrl
      });
    }
  });

  // çµæœã®å‡ºåŠ›
  if (results.length === 0) {
    console.log('ã™ã¹ã¦ã®URLãŒæ­£ã—ãè¨­å®šã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚');
  } else {
    console.log('ä»¥ä¸‹ã®å•é¡ŒãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã—ãŸï¼š\n');
    results.forEach(result => {
      console.log(`ID: ${result.id}`);
      console.log(`ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${result.title}`);
      console.log(`ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: ${result.error}`);
      if (result.currentUrl) console.log(`ç¾åœ¨ã®URL: ${result.currentUrl}`);
      if (result.expectedUrl) console.log(`æœŸå¾…ã•ã‚Œã‚‹URL: ${result.expectedUrl}`);

    });

  console.error('ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãŒç™ºç”Ÿã—ã¾ã—ãŸ:', error);

CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿ã¯æˆåŠŸã—ã¾ã—ãŸãŒã€ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã®æ¯”è¼ƒã«å•é¡ŒãŒã‚ã‚‹ã‚ˆã†ã§ã™ã€‚ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã¨ç‰ˆã®çµ„ã¿åˆã‚ã›ã‚’è€ƒæ…®ã™ã‚‹å¿…è¦ãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™ã€‚ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’ä¿®æ­£ã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```javascript

  // CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿

  const records = parse(csvContent, {
    columns: true,
    skip_empty_lines: true
  });

  // JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
  const jsonData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('../public/data/media-master.json', 'utf8'));

  // ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã¨URLã®ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  const urlMap = new Map();
  records.forEach(record => {
    if (record && record.title) {
      const key = record.edition_type ? 
        `${record.title.trim()} ${record.edition_type.trim()}` : 
        record.title.trim();
      urlMap.set(key, record.url);
    }
  });

  // çµæœã‚’æ ¼ç´ã™ã‚‹é…åˆ—
  const results = [];

  // å„JSONã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒªã‚’ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
  jsonData.forEach(item => {
    const sonyMusicPlatform = item.links.find(link => link.platform === 'sony_music');
    if (!sonyMusicPlatform) {
      return; // sony_musicãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ ãŒãªã„å ´åˆã¯ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒƒãƒ—
    }

    const currentUrl = sonyMusicPlatform.urls.direct;
    const itemTitle = item.edition_name ? 
      `${item.title} ${item.edition_name}` : 
      item.title;
    const csvUrl = urlMap.get(itemTitle);

    if (!currentUrl && csvUrl) {
      results.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: itemTitle,
        error: 'URLãŒæœªè¨­å®šã§ã™',
        expectedUrl: csvUrl
      });
    } else if (currentUrl && !csvUrl) {
      results.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: itemTitle,
        error: 'CSVã«URLãŒå­˜åœ¨ã—ã¾ã›ã‚“',
        currentUrl: currentUrl
      });
    } else if (currentUrl !== csvUrl && csvUrl) {
      results.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: itemTitle,
        error: 'URLãŒä¸€è‡´ã—ã¾ã›ã‚“',
        currentUrl: currentUrl,
        expectedUrl: csvUrl
      });
    }
  });

  // çµæœã®å‡ºåŠ›
  if (results.length === 0) {
    console.log('ã™ã¹ã¦ã®URLãŒæ­£ã—ãè¨­å®šã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚');
  } else {
    console.log('ä»¥ä¸‹ã®å•é¡ŒãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã—ãŸï¼š\n');
    results.forEach(result => {
      console.log(`ID: ${result.id}`);
      console.log(`ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${result.title}`);
      console.log(`ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: ${result.error}`);
      if (result.currentUrl) console.log(`ç¾åœ¨ã®URL: ${result.currentUrl}`);
      if (result.expectedUrl) console.log(`æœŸå¾…ã•ã‚Œã‚‹URL: ${result.expectedUrl}`);
      console.log('---\n');
    });
  }

  // ãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°ç”¨ï¼šãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°ã®å†…å®¹ã‚’è¡¨ç¤º
  console.log('\nãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°æƒ…å ±:');
  console.log('URLãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°:');
  urlMap.forEach((url, title) => {
    console.log(`${title}: ${url}`);
  });

} catch (error) {
  console.error('ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãŒç™ºç”Ÿã—ã¾ã—ãŸ:', error);
}
```

ä¿®æ­£ã—ãŸã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’å®Ÿè¡Œã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’ã•ã‚‰ã«æ”¹å–„ã—ã¦ã€ã‚ˆã‚Šè©³ç´°ãªæƒ…å ±ã‚’è¡¨ç¤ºã™ã‚‹ã‚ˆã†ã«ã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const { parse } = require('csv-parse/sync');

try {
  // CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
  const csvContent = fs.readFileSync('SonyMusicã®å•†å“ä¸€è¦§_VOTE30ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯æ´—ã„å‡ºã—ç”¨.csv', 'utf8');
  const records = parse(csvContent, {
    columns: true,
    skip_empty_lines: true
  });

  // JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
  const jsonData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('../public/data/media-master.json', 'utf8'));

  // ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã¨URLã®ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°ã‚’ä½œæˆ
  const urlMap = new Map();
  records.forEach(record => {
    if (record && record.title) {
      const key = record.edition_type ? 
        `${record.title.trim()} ${record.edition_type.trim()}` : 
        record.title.trim();
      urlMap.set(key, {
        url: record.url,
        media_type: record.media_type
      });
    }
  });

  // çµæœã‚’æ ¼ç´ã™ã‚‹é…åˆ—
  const results = {
    missingUrls: [],
    mismatchedUrls: [],
    missingInCsv: [],
    noSonyMusic: []
  };

  // å„JSONã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒªã‚’ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
  jsonData.forEach(item => {
    const sonyMusicPlatform = item.links.find(link => link.platform === 'sony_music');
    if (!sonyMusicPlatform) {
      results.noSonyMusic.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: item.title,
        edition_name: item.edition_name || ''
      });
      return;
    }

    const currentUrl = sonyMusicPlatform.urls.direct;
    const itemTitle = item.edition_name ? 
      `${item.title} ${item.edition_name}` : 
      item.title;
    const csvData = urlMap.get(itemTitle);

    if (!currentUrl && csvData) {
      results.missingUrls.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: itemTitle,
        expectedUrl: csvData.url,
        media_type: csvData.media_type
      });
    } else if (currentUrl && !csvData) {
      results.missingInCsv.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: itemTitle,
        currentUrl: currentUrl
      });
    } else if (currentUrl !== csvData?.url && csvData) {
      results.mismatchedUrls.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: itemTitle,
        currentUrl: currentUrl,
        expectedUrl: csvData.url,
        media_type: csvData.media_type
      });
    }
  });

  // çµæœã®å‡ºåŠ›
  console.log('ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯çµæœ:\n');

  if (results.missingUrls.length > 0) {
    console.log('1. URLãŒæœªè¨­å®šã®ã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒª:');
    results.missingUrls.forEach(item => {
      console.log(`\nID: ${item.id}`);
      console.log(`ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${item.title}`);
      console.log(`ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—: ${item.media_type}`);
      console.log(`æœŸå¾…ã•ã‚Œã‚‹URL: ${item.expectedUrl}`);
    });
  }

  if (results.mismatchedUrls.length > 0) {
    console.log('\n2. URLãŒä¸€è‡´ã—ãªã„ã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒª:');
    results.mismatchedUrls.forEach(item => {
      console.log(`\nID: ${item.id}`);
      console.log(`ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${item.title}`);
      console.log(`ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—: ${item.media_type}`);
      console.log(`ç¾åœ¨ã®URL: ${item.currentUrl}`);
      console.log(`æœŸå¾…ã•ã‚Œã‚‹URL: ${item.expectedUrl}`);
    });
  }

  if (results.missingInCsv.length > 0) {
    console.log('\n3. CSVã«å­˜åœ¨ã—ãªã„ã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒª:');
    results.missingInCsv.forEach(item => {
      console.log(`\nID: ${item.id}`);
      console.log(`ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${item.title}`);
      console.log(`ç¾åœ¨ã®URL: ${item.currentUrl}`);
    });
  }

  if (results.noSonyMusic.length > 0) {
    console.log('\n4. sony_musicãƒ—ãƒ©ãƒƒãƒˆãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ ãŒè¨­å®šã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ãªã„ã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒª:');
    results.noSonyMusic.forEach(item => {
      console.log(`\nID: ${item.id}`);
      console.log(`ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${item.title}`);
      if (item.edition_name) console.log(`ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³: ${item.edition_name}`);
    });
  }

  if (Object.values(results).every(arr => arr.length === 0)) {
    console.log('ã™ã¹ã¦ã®URLãŒæ­£ã—ãè¨­å®šã•ã‚Œã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚');
  }

  // ãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°ç”¨ï¼šCSVãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°
  console.log('\nãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°æƒ…å ±:');
  console.log('CSVãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°:');
  urlMap.forEach((data, title) => {
    console.log(`\nã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${title}`);
    console.log(`URL: ${data.url}`);
    console.log(`ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—: ${data.media_type}`);
  });

} catch (error) {
  console.error('ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãŒç™ºç”Ÿã—ã¾ã—ãŸ:', error);
}

æ”¹å–„ã—ãŸã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’å®Ÿè¡Œã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

çµæœã‚’åˆ†æã™ã‚‹ã¨ã€ä»¥ä¸‹ã®ã‚ˆã†ãªå•é¡ŒãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã—ãŸï¼š

1. ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã®è¡¨è¨˜ã®é•ã„ï¼š
   - JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã¨CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã§ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã®è¡¨è¨˜ãŒç•°ãªã‚‹å ´åˆãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™
   - ä¾‹ï¼š`DOUBLE-DEALå®Œå…¨ç”Ÿç”£é™å®šç›¤A` vs `DOUBLE-DEAL ã€å®Œå…¨ç”Ÿç”£é™å®šç›¤/Aã€‘`

2. ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³åã®è¡¨è¨˜ã®é•ã„ï¼š
   - æ‹¬å¼§ã®ç¨®é¡ã‚„ç©ºç™½ã®æœ‰ç„¡ãŒç•°ãªã‚Šã¾ã™
   - ä¾‹ï¼š`ï¼ˆé€šå¸¸ç›¤ï¼‰` vs `ã€é€šå¸¸ç›¤ã€‘`

ã“ã‚Œã‚‰ã®å•é¡Œã‚’è§£æ±ºã™ã‚‹ãŸã‚ã«ã€ä»¥ä¸‹ã®å¯¾ç­–ã‚’ææ¡ˆã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

1. ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã¨ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³åã®æ­£è¦åŒ–ï¼š
   - ç©ºç™½ã‚’çµ±ä¸€
   - æ‹¬å¼§ã®ç¨®é¡ã‚’çµ±ä¸€
   - ç‰¹æ®Šæ–‡å­—ã®è¡¨è¨˜ã‚’çµ±ä¸€

2. ä¸€æ‹¬ä¿®æ­£ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã®ä½œæˆï¼š
   - CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’åŸºæº–ã¨ã—ã¦ã€JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®URLã‚’æ›´æ–°
   - ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã¨ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³åã®ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«ã‚’ä½œæˆ

ã¾ãšã€ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã®æ­£è¦åŒ–ã‚’è¡Œã†ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const { parse } = require('csv-parse/sync');

// ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã‚’æ­£è¦åŒ–ã™ã‚‹é–¢æ•°
function normalizeTitle(title) {
  return title
    .replace(/['']/g, "'")  // ã‚¢ãƒã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ­ãƒ•ã‚£ã®çµ±ä¸€
    .replace(/[""]/g, '"')  // ã‚¯ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒˆã®çµ±ä¸€
    .replace(/[â…¡]/g, 'II') // ãƒ­ãƒ¼ãƒæ•°å­—ã®çµ±ä¸€
    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')   // è¤‡æ•°ã®ç©ºç™½ã‚’1ã¤ã«
    .trim();               // å‰å¾Œã®ç©ºç™½ã‚’å‰Šé™¤
}

// ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³åã‚’æ­£è¦åŒ–ã™ã‚‹é–¢æ•°
function normalizeEdition(edition) {
  if (!edition) return '';
  return edition
    .replace(/[ï¼ˆï¼‰]/g, match => match === 'ï¼ˆ' ? 'ã€' : 'ã€‘') // æ‹¬å¼§ã®çµ±ä¸€
    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')   // è¤‡æ•°ã®ç©ºç™½ã‚’1ã¤ã«
    .trim();               // å‰å¾Œã®ç©ºç™½ã‚’å‰Šé™¤
}

try {
  // CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
  const csvContent = fs.readFileSync('SonyMusicã®å•†å“ä¸€è¦§_VOTE30ãƒªãƒ³ã‚¯æ´—ã„å‡ºã—ç”¨.csv', 'utf8');
  const records = parse(csvContent, {
    columns: true,
    skip_empty_lines: true
  });

  // JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã®èª­ã¿è¾¼ã¿
  const jsonData = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync('../public/data/media-master.json', 'utf8'));

  // ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°ãƒ†ãƒ¼ãƒ–ãƒ«ã®ä½œæˆ
  const titleMap = new Map();
  records.forEach(record => {
    if (record && record.title) {
      const normalizedTitle = normalizeTitle(record.title);
      const normalizedEdition = normalizeEdition(record.edition_type);
      const key = normalizedEdition ? 
        `${normalizedTitle} ${normalizedEdition}` : 
        normalizedTitle;
      
      titleMap.set(key, {
        originalTitle: record.title,
        originalEdition: record.edition_type,
        url: record.url,
        media_type: record.media_type
      });
    }
  });

  // JSONãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã®å„ã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒªã‚’ãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯
  const results = {
    matched: [],
    unmatched: []
  };

  jsonData.forEach(item => {
    const sonyMusicPlatform = item.links.find(link => link.platform === 'sony_music');
    if (!sonyMusicPlatform) return;

    const normalizedTitle = normalizeTitle(item.title);
    const normalizedEdition = normalizeEdition(item.edition_name || '');
    const key = normalizedEdition ? 
      `${normalizedTitle} ${normalizedEdition}` : 
      normalizedTitle;

    const matchedData = titleMap.get(key);
    if (matchedData) {
      results.matched.push({
        id: item.id,
        jsonTitle: item.title,
        jsonEdition: item.edition_name,
        csvTitle: matchedData.originalTitle,
        csvEdition: matchedData.originalEdition,
        normalizedKey: key,
        url: matchedData.url
      });
    } else {
      results.unmatched.push({
        id: item.id,
        title: item.title,
        edition: item.edition_name,
        normalizedKey: key,
        currentUrl: sonyMusicPlatform.urls.direct
      });
    }
  });

  // çµæœã®å‡ºåŠ›
  console.log('ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«æ­£è¦åŒ–ã®çµæœ:\n');

  if (results.matched.length > 0) {
    console.log('1. ãƒãƒƒãƒã—ãŸã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒª:');
    results.matched.forEach(item => {
      console.log(`\nID: ${item.id}`);
      console.log(`JSONå´ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${item.jsonTitle}`);
      if (item.jsonEdition) console.log(`JSONå´ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³: ${item.jsonEdition}`);
      console.log(`CSVå´ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${item.csvTitle}`);
      if (item.csvEdition) console.log(`CSVå´ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³: ${item.csvEdition}`);
      console.log(`æ­£è¦åŒ–ã‚­ãƒ¼: ${item.normalizedKey}`);
      console.log(`URL: ${item.url}`);
    });
  }

  if (results.unmatched.length > 0) {
    console.log('\n2. ãƒãƒƒãƒã—ãªã‹ã£ãŸã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒª:');
    results.unmatched.forEach(item => {
      console.log(`\nID: ${item.id}`);
      console.log(`ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${item.title}`);
      if (item.edition) console.log(`ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³: ${item.edition}`);
      console.log(`æ­£è¦åŒ–ã‚­ãƒ¼: ${item.normalizedKey}`);
      console.log(`ç¾åœ¨ã®URL: ${item.currentUrl}`);
    });
  }

  // ãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°ç”¨ï¼šæ­£è¦åŒ–ã•ã‚ŒãŸã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã®ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°
  console.log('\nãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°æƒ…å ±:');
  console.log('æ­£è¦åŒ–ã•ã‚ŒãŸã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã®ãƒãƒƒãƒ”ãƒ³ã‚°:');
  titleMap.forEach((data, key) => {
    console.log(`\næ­£è¦åŒ–ã‚­ãƒ¼: ${key}`);
    console.log(`ã‚ªãƒªã‚¸ãƒŠãƒ«ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«: ${data.originalTitle}`);
    if (data.originalEdition) console.log(`ã‚ªãƒªã‚¸ãƒŠãƒ«ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³: ${data.originalEdition}`);
    console.log(`URL: ${data.url}`);
    console.log(`ãƒ¡ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚¢ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒ—: ${data.media_type}`);
  });

} catch (error) {
  console.error('ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãŒç™ºç”Ÿã—ã¾ã—ãŸ:', error);
}
```

æ­£è¦åŒ–ã‚¹ã‚¯ãƒªãƒ—ãƒˆã‚’å®Ÿè¡Œã—ã¦ã¿ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ï¼š

çµæœã‚’åˆ†æã™ã‚‹ã¨ã€ä»¥ä¸‹ã®ã‚ˆã†ãªå•é¡ŒãŒè¦‹ã¤ã‹ã‚Šã¾ã—ãŸï¼š

1. ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã®è¡¨è¨˜ã®é•ã„ï¼š
   - ç‰¹æ®Šæ–‡å­—ï¼ˆãƒã‚¤ãƒ•ãƒ³ã€ã‚¢ãƒã‚¹ãƒˆãƒ­ãƒ•ã‚£ã€æ‹¬å¼§ãªã©ï¼‰ã®è¡¨è¨˜ãŒç•°ãªã‚‹
   - ç©ºç™½ã®æœ‰ç„¡ãŒç•°ãªã‚‹
   - å¤§æ–‡å­—å°æ–‡å­—ã®é•ã„

2. ã‚¨ãƒ‡ã‚£ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³åã®è¡¨è¨˜ã®é•ã„ï¼š
   - æ‹¬å¼§ã®ç¨®é¡ï¼ˆã€ã€‘vsï¼ˆï¼‰ï¼‰
   - ã‚¹ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¹ã®æœ‰ç„¡
   - åŒºåˆ‡ã‚Šæ–‡å­—ï¼ˆ/ã‚„-ï¼‰ã®é•ã„

3. æœªç™»éŒ²ã®ã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒªï¼š
   - CSVãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã«å­˜åœ¨ã—ãªã„ã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒªãŒã‚ã‚‹
   - JSONãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã«å­˜åœ¨ã—ãªã„ã‚¨ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒªãŒã‚ã‚‹

ã“ã‚Œã‚‰ã®å•é¡Œã‚’è§£æ±ºã™ã‚‹ãŸã‚ã«ã€ä»¥ä¸‹ã®å¯¾ç­–ã‚’ææ¡ˆã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

1. ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã®æ­£è¦åŒ–ãƒ«ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã®æ”¹å–„ï¼š
